<pr_description>
MapLibre mutates projection object when json passed to `setStyle`
**maplibre-gl-js version**: 5.6.0

**browser**: all

We rely on passing a js object to set styles in our style editor. We were having trouble changing projections by passing a JSON object. I initially thought there was a problem with our SDK (which extends ML Map) but upon digging deeper, I discovered the problem in ML

### Steps to Trigger Behavior

 1. navigate to demo
 2. observe styles in html source are passed as a js object,
 3. change styles
 4. observe that the original stylesheet is mutated

### Link to Demonstration

https://jsbin.com/gakuliy/1/edit?html,output

### Expected Behavior
Maplibre should not mutate the stylesheet that is passed.

### Actual Behavior
Maplibre internally mutates the stylesheet that is passed.

Some additional notes:
- I was also passing the styles through `structuredClone` before passing them to `setStyle`, this fixed the change from mercator to globe and back, but the stylesheet object is still mutated.
- when no projection is passed as part of the style, the projection does not default to mercator and remains the same (and subsequently does not fire a `projectiontransition` event), is this the expected behaviour or is it expected to always default back to mercator if no projection is passed in the style?

</pr_description>

   119	/**
   120	 * Part of {@link Map.setStyle} options, transformStyle is a convenience function that allows to modify a style after it is fetched but before it is committed to the map state.
   121	 *
   122	 * This function exposes previous and next styles, it can be commonly used to support a range of functionalities like:
   123	 *
   124	 * - when previous style carries certain 'state' that needs to be carried over to a new style gracefully;
   125	 * - when a desired style is a certain combination of previous and incoming style;
   126	 * - when an incoming style requires modification based on external state.
   127	 * - when an incoming style uses relative paths, which need to be converted to absolute.
   128	 *
   129	 * @param previous - The current style.
   130	 * @param next - The next style.
   131	 * @returns resulting style that will to be applied to the map
   132	 *
   133	 * @example
   134	 * ```ts
   135	 * map.setStyle('https://demotiles.maplibre.org/style.json', {
   136	 *   transformStyle: (previousStyle, nextStyle) => ({
   137	 *       ...nextStyle,
   138	 *       // make relative sprite path like "../sprite" absolute
   139	 *       sprite: new URL(nextStyle.sprite, "https://demotiles.maplibre.org/styles/osm-bright-gl-style/sprites/").href,
   140	 *       // make relative glyphs path like "../fonts/{fontstack}/{range}.pbf" absolute
   141	 *       glyphs: new URL(nextStyle.glyphs, "https://demotiles.maplibre.org/font/").href,
   142	 *       sources: {
   143	 *           // make relative vector url like "../../" absolute
   144	 *           ...nextStyle.sources.map(source => {
   145	 *              if (source.url) {
   146	 *                  source.url = new URL(source.url, "https://api.maptiler.com/tiles/osm-bright-gl-style/");
   147	 *              }
   148	 *              return source;
   149	 *           }),
   150	 *           // copy a source from previous style
   151	 *           'osm': previousStyle.sources.osm
   152	 *       },
   153	 *       layers: [
   154	 *           // background layer
   155	 *           nextStyle.layers[0],
   156	 *           // copy a layer from previous style
   157	 *           previousStyle.layers[0],
   158	 *           // other layers from the next style
   159	 *           ...nextStyle.layers.slice(1).map(layer => {
   160	 *               // hide the layers we don't need from demotiles style
   161	 *               if (layer.id.startsWith('geolines')) {
   162	 *                   layer.layout = {...layer.layout || {}, visibility: 'none'};
   163	 *               // filter out US polygons
   164	 *               } else if (layer.id.startsWith('coastline') || layer.id.startsWith('countries')) {
   165	 *                   layer.filter = ['!=', ['get', 'ADM0_A3'], 'USA'];
   166	 *               }
   167	 *               return layer;
   168	 *           })
   169	 *       ]
   170	 *   })
   171	 * });
   172	 * ```
   173	 */
   174	export type TransformStyleFunction = (previous: StyleSpecification | undefined, next: StyleSpecification) => StyleSpecification;

   234	    crossTileSymbolIndex: CrossTileSymbolIndex;
   235	    pauseablePlacement: PauseablePlacement;

   238	
   239	    constructor(map: Map, options: StyleOptions = {}) {
   240	        super();
   241	
   242	        this.map = map;
   243	        this.dispatcher = new Dispatcher(getGlobalWorkerPool(), map._getMapId());
   244	        this.dispatcher.registerMessageHandler(MessageType.getGlyphs, (mapId, params) => {
   245	            return this.getGlyphs(mapId, params);
   246	        });
   247	        this.dispatcher.registerMessageHandler(MessageType.getImages, (mapId, params) => {
   248	            return this.getImages(mapId, params);
   249	        });
   250	        this.imageManager = new ImageManager();
   251	        this.imageManager.setEventedParent(this);
   252	        this.glyphManager = new GlyphManager(map._requestManager, options.localIdeographFontFamily);
   253	        this.lineAtlas = new LineAtlas(256, 512);
   254	        this.crossTileSymbolIndex = new CrossTileSymbolIndex();
   255	
   256	        this._spritesImagesIds = {};
   257	        this._layers = {};
   258	
   259	        this._order = [];
   260	        this.sourceCaches = {};
   261	        this.zoomHistory = new ZoomHistory();
   262	        this._loaded = false;
   263	        this._availableImages = [];
   264	        this._globalState = {};
   265	
   266	        this._resetUpdates();
   267	
   268	        this.dispatcher.broadcast(MessageType.setReferrer, getReferrer());
   269	        rtlMainThreadPluginFactory().on(RTLPluginLoadedEventName, this._rtlPluginLoaded);
   270	
   271	        this.on('data', (event) => {
   272	            if (event.dataType !== 'source' || event.sourceDataType !== 'metadata') {
   273	                return;
   274	            }
   275	
   276	            const sourceCache = this.sourceCaches[event.sourceId];
   277	            if (!sourceCache) {
   278	                return;
   279	            }
   280	
   281	            const source = sourceCache.getSource();
   282	            if (!source || !source.vectorLayerIds) {
   283	                return;
   284	            }
   285	
   286	            for (const layerId in this._layers) {
   287	                const layer = this._layers[layerId];
   288	                if (layer.source === source.id) {
   289	                    this._validateLayer(layer);
   290	                }
   291	            }
   292	        });
   293	    }
   294	
   295	    _rtlPluginLoaded = () => {
   296	        for (const id in this.sourceCaches) {
   297	            const sourceType = this.sourceCaches[id].getSource().type;
   298	            if (sourceType === 'vector' || sourceType === 'geojson') {
   299	                // Non-vector sources don't have any symbols buckets to reload when the RTL text plugin loads
   300	                // They also load more quickly, so they're more likely to have already displaying tiles
   301	                // that would be unnecessarily booted by the plugin load event
   302	                this.sourceCaches[id].reload(); // Should be a no-op if the plugin loads before any tiles load
   303	            }
   304	        }
   305	    };
   306	
   307	    setGlobalStateProperty(name: string, value: any) {
   308	        this._checkLoaded();
   309	
   310	        const newValue = value === null ?
   311	            this.stylesheet.state?.[name]?.default ?? null :
   312	            value;
   313	
   314	        if (deepEqual(newValue, this._globalState[name])) {
   315	            return this;
   316	        }
   317	
   318	        this._globalState[name] = newValue;
   319	
   320	        const sourceIdsToReload = this._findGlobalStateAffectedSources([name]);
   321	
   322	        for (const id in this.sourceCaches) {
   323	            if (sourceIdsToReload.has(id)) {
   324	                this._reloadSource(id);
   325	                this._changed = true;
   326	            }
   327	        }
   328	    }
   329	
   330	    getGlobalState() {
   331	        return this._globalState;
   332	    }
   333	
   334	    setGlobalState(newStylesheetState: StateSpecification) {
   335	        this._checkLoaded();
   336	
   337	        const changedGlobalStateRefs = [];
   338	
   339	        for (const propertyName in newStylesheetState) {
   340	            const didChange = !deepEqual(this._globalState[propertyName], newStylesheetState[propertyName].default);
   341	
   342	            if (didChange) {
   343	                changedGlobalStateRefs.push(propertyName);
   344	                this._globalState[propertyName] = newStylesheetState[propertyName].default;
   345	            }

   354	            }
   355	        }
   356	    }
   357	
   358	    /**
   359	     * Find all sources that are affected by the global state changes.
   360	     * For example, if a layer filter uses global-state expression, this function will return the source id of that layer.
   361	     */
   362	    _findGlobalStateAffectedSources(globalStateRefs: string[]) {
   363	        if (globalStateRefs.length === 0) {
   364	            return new Set<string>();
   365	        }
   366	
   367	        const sourceIdsToReload = new Set<string>();

   376	                }
   377	            }
   378	        }
   379	
   380	        return sourceIdsToReload;
   381	    }

   419	    _load(json: StyleSpecification, options: StyleSwapOptions & StyleSetterOptions, previousStyle?: StyleSpecification) {
   420	        const nextState = options.transformStyle ? options.transformStyle(previousStyle, json) : json;
   421	        if (options.validate && emitValidationErrors(this, validateStyle(nextState))) {
   422	            return;
   423	        }
   424	
   425	        this._loaded = true;
   426	        this.stylesheet = nextState;
   427	
   428	        for (const id in nextState.sources) {
   429	            this.addSource(id, nextState.sources[id], {validate: false});
   430	        }
   431	
   432	        if (nextState.sprite) {
   433	            this._loadSprite(nextState.sprite);
   434	        } else {
   435	            this.imageManager.setLoaded(true);
   436	        }
   437	
   438	        this.glyphManager.setURL(nextState.glyphs);
   439	        this._createLayers();
   440	
   441	        this.light = new Light(this.stylesheet.light);
   442	        this._setProjectionInternal(this.stylesheet.projection?.type || 'mercator');
   443	
   444	        this.sky = new Sky(this.stylesheet.sky);
   445	
   446	        this.map.setTerrain(this.stylesheet.terrain ?? null);
   447	
   448	        this.setGlobalState(this.stylesheet.state ?? null);
   449	
   450	        this.fire(new Event('data', {dataType: 'style'}));
   451	        this.fire(new Event('style.load'));
   452	    }

     1	import type {CanonicalTileID} from '../../source/tile_id';
     2	import type {PreparedShader} from '../../shaders/shaders';
     3	import type {Context} from '../../gl/context';
     4	import type {Mesh} from '../../render/mesh';
     5	import type {Program} from '../../render/program';
     6	import type {SubdivisionGranularitySetting} from '../../render/subdivision_granularity_settings';
     7	import type {ProjectionSpecification} from '@maplibre/maplibre-gl-style-spec';
     8	import type {EvaluationParameters} from '../../style/evaluation_parameters';
     9	
    10	/**
    11	 * Custom projections are handled both by a class which implements this `Projection` interface,
    12	 * and a class that is derived from the `Transform` base class. What is the difference?
    13	 *
    14	 * The transform-derived class:
    15	 * - should do all the heavy lifting for the projection - implement all the `project*` and `unproject*` functions, etc.
    16	 * - must store the map's state - center, pitch, etc. - this is handled in the `Transform` base class
    17	 * - must be cloneable - it should not create any heavy resources
    18	 *
    19	 * The projection-implementing class:
    20	 * - must provide basic information and data about the projection, which is *independent of the map's state* - name, shader functions, subdivision settings, etc.
    21	 * - must be a "singleton" - no matter how many copies of the matching Transform class exist, the Projection should always exist as a single instance (per Map)
    22	 * - may create heavy resources that should not exist in multiple copies (projection is never cloned) - for example, see the GPU inaccuracy mitigation for globe projection
    23	 * - must be explicitly disposed of after usage using the `destroy` function - this allows the implementing class to free any allocated resources
    24	 */
    25	
    26	/**
    27	 * @internal
    28	 */
    29	export type ProjectionGPUContext = {
    30	    context: Context;
    31	    useProgram: (name: string) => Program<any>;
    32	};
    33	
    34	/**
    35	 * @internal
    36	 * Specifies the usage for a square tile mesh:
    37	 * - 'stencil' for drawing stencil masks
    38	 * - 'raster' for drawing raster tiles, hillshade, etc.
    39	 */
    40	export type TileMeshUsage = 'stencil' | 'raster';
    41	
    42	/**
    43	 * An interface the implementations of which are used internally by MapLibre to handle different projections.
    44	 */
    45	export interface Projection {
    46	    /**
    47	     * @internal
    48	     * A short, descriptive name of this projection, such as 'mercator' or 'globe'.
    49	     */
    50	    get name(): ProjectionSpecification['type'];
    51	
    52	    /**
    53	     * @internal
    54	     * True if this projection needs to render subdivided geometry.
    55	     * Optimized rendering paths for non-subdivided geometry might be used throughout MapLibre.
    56	     * The value of this property may change during runtime, for example in globe projection depending on zoom.
    57	     */
    58	    get useSubdivision(): boolean;
    59	
    60	    /**
    61	     * Name of the shader projection variant that should be used for this projection.
    62	     * Note that this value may change dynamically, for example when globe projection internally transitions to mercator.
    63	     * Then globe projection might start reporting the mercator shader variant name to make MapLibre use faster mercator shaders.
    64	     */
    65	    get shaderVariantName(): string;

    71	     */
    72	    get shaderDefine(): string;

    90	     */

    31	    constructor() {

    33	    }
    34

    36	        value: PropertyValue<[number, number, number], LightPosition>,
    37	        parameters: EvaluationParameters
    38	    ): LightPosition {
    39	        return sphericalToCartesian(value.expression.evaluate(parameters));
    40	    }

    42	    interpolate(a: LightPosition, b: LightPosition, t: number): LightPosition {

    69	/*
    70	 * Represents the light used to light extruded features.
    71	 */
    72	export class Light extends Evented {
    73	    _transitionable: Transitionable<LightProps>;
    74	    _transitioning: Transitioning<LightProps>;
    75	    properties: PossiblyEvaluated<LightProps, LightPropsPossiblyEvaluated>;
    76	
    77	    constructor(lightOptions?: LightSpecification) {
    78	        super();
    79	        lightProperties = lightProperties || new Properties({
    80	            'anchor': new DataConstantProperty(styleSpec.light.anchor as StylePropertySpecification),
    81	            'position': new LightPositionProperty(),
    82	            'color': new DataConstantProperty(styleSpec.light.color as StylePropertySpecification),
    83	            'intensity': new DataConstantProperty(styleSpec.light.intensity as StylePropertySpecification),
    84	        });
    85	        this._transitionable = new Transitionable(lightProperties);
    86	        this.setLight(lightOptions);
    87	        this._transitioning = this._transitionable.untransitioned();
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    getLight(): LightSpecification {
    91	        return this._transitionable.serialize();
    92	    }
    93	
    94	    setLight(light?: LightSpecification, options: StyleSetterOptions = {}) {
    95	        if (this._validate(validateLight, light, options)) {
    96	            return;
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        for (const name in light) {
   100	            const value = light[name];
   101	            if (name.endsWith(TRANSITION_SUFFIX)) {
   102	                this._transitionable.setTransition(name.slice(0, -TRANSITION_SUFFIX.length) as keyof LightProps, value);
   103	            } else {
   104	                this._transitionable.setValue(name as keyof LightProps, value);
   105	            }
   106	        }
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    updateTransitions(parameters: TransitionParameters) {
   110	        this._transitioning = this._transitionable.transitioned(parameters, this._transitioning);
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    hasTransition() {
   114	        return this._transitioning.hasTransition();
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    recalculate(parameters: EvaluationParameters) {
   118	        this.properties = this._transitioning.possiblyEvaluate(parameters);
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    _validate(validate: Function, value: unknown, options?: {
   122	        validate?: boolean;
   123	    }) {
   124	        if (options && options.validate === false) {
   125	            return false;
   126	        }
